    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_42beeb89-6236-4b9b-b49a-db2090e020df'

  <span id="freeText22536115200997613" style="display:none">Marie doesn’t need a complication like Horse. The massive, tattooed, badass biker who shows up at her brother’s house one afternoon doesn’t agree. He wants Marie on his bike and in his bed. Now.<br /><br />But Marie just left her abusive jerk of an ex-husband and she’s not looking for a new man. Especially one like Horse—she doesn’t know his real name or where he lives, she’s ninety percent certain he’s a criminal and that the “business” he talks with her brother isn’t website design. She needs him out of her life, which would be a snap if he’d just stop giving her mind-blowing orgasms.<br /><br />Horse is part of the Reapers Motorcycle Club, and when he wants something, he takes it. What he wants is Marie, but she’s not interested in becoming “property of”.<br /><br />Then her brother steals from the club. Marie can save him by giving Horse what he wants—at home, in public, on his bike… If she’s a very, very good girl, she’ll get lots more of those orgasms only he can offer, and he’ll let her brother live.<br />Maybe.</span>

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});
        } else {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('edition_17256900').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('edition_17256900').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });

  <span id="freeText5836227899939860132" style="display:none"><b>*****WOOT! I just saw that Reaper's Property is the 500th book that I have rated on GR!*****</b><br><br><b>4 yummy stars.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1071.beta.photobucket.com/user/MsBaba4/media/tattoos_piercings/Bildschirmfoto2013-01-17um183941_zps7bc8985d.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>After leaving her abusive and cheating husband, Marie is living with her brother in a trailer. Jeff is working for the Reapers, a motorcycle club. Marie and Horse kind of hook up when Horse and his brothers are visiting Jeff to discuss business. Later on, Horse offers Marie an exclusive relationship with him; he wanted her to be his <i>old lady,</i> but she refused flat out and on top of that, she even insulted him and hurt his feelings. Marie totally blew him off and they stopped talking and things went downhill. Our heroine got drunk, sent him a bunch of stupid texts and from there on things fell really apart. Now back to dear ole Jeff who has gotten himself into real trouble…<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Why don't I buy her?" Horse said. Everyone turned to look at him, startled. "I'll buy Marie from the club, and we give Jensen another shot. Fifty grand, outta my pocket and into the club account. We wait and see if Jensen comes up with the money and interest. He does, I get paid back, the club makes a profit. He doesn't, it's on me."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>When Marie found the Reapers holding a gun to her brother's head she did accept Horse's "offer" that if she would go with him they would give Jeff another chance to put things right. Unfortunately though, our innocent heroine is clueless and she is so in for it.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"You do this, it's your choice. I'm not raping you. You're making a decision to pay for your brother's mistake on your back. </a><br><br>Marie had fallen into a new, strange, and unknown world where people didn't follow the rules. They live in a different world with different rules. That's the reality in the MC world. To top it all off, it's a very sexist world. But instead of feeling horrified at what she was seeing and experiencing, Marie actually "liked" her new life. Horse wanted to claim Marie and he didn't want to share her with his brothers. Claiming a woman, branding her as his property meant that she would be untouchable.<br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"A man takes a woman, means to keep her, she becomes his property," Horse continued. "We covered that before--it's a sign of commitment, of respect. It means he'll protect her and everyone else better keep their fucking hands off her or be ready to fight him and his brothers. You do not want to fuck with a man's old lady."</blockquote>
  </b>

The hero is called Horse because he is hung like a…<br><br><a href="http://s1071.beta.photobucket.com/user/MsBaba4/media/gifs/tumblr_lzbe9wipWH1qg4j5bo1_500_large_zps1c14510e.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And let's just get it out of the way: Reaper's Property is not a KA copy. There are very few quotes that are similar to KA speech but that's about it.<br><br>There's plenty of explicit sex and you are getting your money's worth, that's for sure. While the sex scenes are well-written and steamy, some are a bit rough but nothing OTT. </a><br><br>Granted, the hero had a couple of asshat moments to work through and that was mainly Marie's fault. On the other hand I was pleased to see how sweet, tender, and caring Horse could be. In all fairness I have to say that Horse saying offensive things was understandable and he redeemed himself along the way. Even though I love to read about this lifestyle I'm very sure it would never work out for me in real life. All this archaic behavior is so not for me and I'm certainly not into illegal stuff either. Nobody is going to own me, nobody is going to tell me when and where I have to spread my legs and nobody is telling me what I have to do in the house. Nope. It would not suit me at all. All things considered though, I can understand why it would appeal to other <s>people</s> women. Still, it's always too romanticized in books but I think it's all right. Horse is a good example why I love to read about a badass biker hero. Let's just have a good time!<br><br><b>What didn't quite work for me</b><br>The timeframe hopping was <b>irritating.</b> Furthermore, I found it rather stupid when Marie asked <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Max to give her and Cookie a ride home. In fact, the plot twist regarding the betrayal which led to the final shootout was too predictable. On top of that, I never liked Max and I'd be lying if I'd say that I was surprised to see him end up on the wrong path. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Once again we have a lack of communication and/or miscommunication. To be honest, it's becoming a little pet peeve of mine. Marie really annoyed me when she was jumping to conclusions instead of addressing her issues.<br><br>Finally, the epilogue was a little bit too saccharine for my liking even though I loved Horse's <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[proposal. That was well done and fun. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><i>Reaper's Property</i> is not without flaws, but overall it's a very entertaining read. One thing's for sure, there's never a dull moment to be found. Plenty of colorful characters, hot sex, some nice action, and little bit of drama kicked some serious ass! If you don't mind to read about sexist behavior and men who make their own rules in life then give it a try. And last but not least the hero is so darn <s>
  <b>lickable</b>
</s> likable.<br><br><a href="http://s1071.beta.photobucket.com/user/MsBaba4/media/tattoos_piercings/Bildschirmfoto2013-01-19um155351_zps7ab43d6e.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405403i/789666.png" alt=" photo Bildschirmfoto2013-01-19um155351_zps7ab43d6e.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Love you, babe. Are you still planning to shoot me?"</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><br><br><br><i>
  <b>Recommended to readers who loved Kristen Ashley's Motorcycle Man. Also, those readers who didn't particularly like Madeline Sheehan's Undeniable might enjoy Reaper's Property because it's much tamer than <i>Undeniable</i> and there is no <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[rape or cheating. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br></b>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer516431455" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16476926487722619953"><blockquote>
  <b>ROMANCE NOVEL FAIL.</b>
</blockquote> Please note that I am not saying BOOK FAIL or STORY FAIL. I'm only taking issue with the romanticizing of things which should never be romanticized (in a contemporary) without some sort of heavy disclaimer or taboo label. I would have been easier on this book if it had been marketed as taboo and written from the point of view of challenging the reader's perceptions. But this is even labeled as romantica. So FAIL it is.<br/><br/>Some spoilers ahead and a slight bit of swearing. I'm </span>
  <span id="freeText16476926487722619953" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>ROMANCE NOVEL FAIL.</b>
</blockquote> Please note that I am not saying BOOK FAIL or STORY FAIL. I'm only taking issue with the romanticizing of things which should never be romanticized (in a contemporary) without some sort of heavy disclaimer or taboo label. I would have been easier on this book if it had been marketed as taboo and written from the point of view of challenging the reader's perceptions. But this is even labeled as romantica. So FAIL it is.<br><br>Some spoilers ahead and a slight bit of swearing. I'm not in the mood to have to censor myself or try to figure out how to write a polite review which doesn't reveal too much. All bets are off today. Read on at your own peril.<br><br>If I see one more representation of a biker who is an oiled-up, hair-free model posing on a bike that no MC member would be caught dead on, I'm probably going to scream. <br><br>We're talking about a Motorcycle Club, right?<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406660i/793696.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As well, the next time I see anyone bitching about Twilight for being stalker-rific, i'm going to ask if they've read any of the recent "alpha biker" books to have come out. At this point, I'm going to start referring to a vampire watching someone sleep as the more cuddly version of stalking. Because right about now, that behavior seems downright endearing compared to being blackmailed and/or kidnapped and forced to have to become someone's fuck-buddy. <br><br><b>ARE YOU KIDDING ME?</b> <br><br>It's not okay, people. It's not cute. It's not romantic. It's not sexy. Any guy who thinks he's doing you a favor by trading your brothers life for your sexual favors is NOT WORTH DROOLING OVER.<br><br>Wow, I didn't realize how much my switch had been flipped until I started writing this review. In so many ways, this book was a thousand times better than <i>Undeniable</i>. In all honesty, the writing was much more polished and the story had a clearer PoV that wasn't flailing all over the place like it was in Undeniable. Hell, I even think Horse was genuinely more likable than Deuce when looking at the big picture. <br><br>Unfortunately, it was the initial setup for this story which screwed <i>everything</i> up. The book starts off with Marie (one of the dumbest characters I've read to date) frothing at the mouth over a guy for reasons unknown. At least with Undeniable, the chick was raised in the MC world and being treated like this was what she knew and expected, so I wasn't going to rip on someone for staying in a familiar cycle (i.e. crime begets crime). That situation was still ridiculous but it was more understandable.<br><br>But Marie...ridiculous, clueless, brain-dead Marie...<br><br>Yes, I get it - he's hot. <br>Yes, I get it - he's hot.<br>YES, I GET IT - he's hot. <br><br>Right now, I'm ashamed to be a woman, if this is what we've evolved into - frothing at the mouth over a man who is disrespecting you with his words and is rape-y with his actions. Just because a person doesn't physically force someone to have sex with them does not mean that the situation isn't rape. Marie was FORCED into the situation (okay, so she went like a willing, whipped puppy dog...but only after being told that this was her fate, else her brother face the wrath of the Reapers). <br><br>Plus, he punched her wall and broke her door after she said no. For a moment, I was almost happy that Marie was standing up for herself by telling him no. But then, the moment passed because she then laid down and took it like a pro. Sure, she was forced into a bad situation. But she sure seemed to be enjoying it. Was she ever really disgusted by this man who turned her into his own personal sex slave? Because if she was, I never bought into it. Even in her thoughts, she was never really all that disturbed. <br><br>Yet, even with me saying that, I actually liked Horse to a certain extent. He is one of those people who you want to root for <i>as a reader</i>, even though he was a screwed-up person. Yes, he was completely off-base for what he did, but we got to see his side of things and were able to (somewhat) understand where his though process was at when we were in his head. Yes, he acted rape-y in a roundabout way and I didn't like that. But any time he thought he might actually hurt Marie, he did show remorse for it. But Marie wasn't seeing what we were seeing all of the time. She didn't know that he was conflicted. She only accepted what she was given with not enough feelings of 'ewwww' over what she was being put through. Even if she was forced to have to go along with it all, wouldn't the fact that she was being forced be enough to make her slow her roll at least a little?<br><br>Therefore, I found Marie to be completely uh...what's the way to describe her? <br><br>Oh yeah - this. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406660i/793697.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>How can a woman be constantly in heat over a man who hadn't proved himself worthy of her affection?<br><br>Oh right, I know why. Because he was hot. <br><br>Excuse for a moment me while I crawl into a corner and cry for humanity. <br><br>There's a reason why I love the show Sons of Anarchy (hint : it has nothing to do with being a romance). I like watching shit hit the fan. And for that reason, I did find this book to be entertaining. <br><br>And again - if Marie had at least started out more resistant, I could have possibly handled a story in which two people overcome a bad situation and find a way to make things work. I'm okay with "big baddies" being redeemed in many cases. Horse did have a soft side in there somewhere. But he never really had to pay for his actions.<br><br><b>The Marie Dumbass Hall of Fame</b><br><br><i>Even scary, the man made my panties wet.</i><br>~Pssst...Marie. He's scary for a reason. It involves unapologetic violence and killing.<br><br><i>I swayed a little as he stopped, reaching out with one finger to trace my collarbone from my shoulder inward, then running it down between my breasts, grazing the sides. He raised it to his mouth, tasting my sweat. He smelled like motor oil and sex.<br>Holy shit.<br>"Hey, sweet butt," he said.</i><br>~ THIS IS THE VERY FIRST MEETING. Within a few minutes, she was wondering how she could stop herself from pushing her breasts in his face. Classy broad, this one.<br><br><i>I'm ashamed to admit that I creamed my pants right then and there instead of kicking him in the nuts like a sensible girl.</i><br>~ First off, gross. I don't want to know about your discharge, woman. Secondly, she's aware that she's being stupid. Oh right...hot man trumps all.<br><br><i>Part of me wondered if Horse had come back. You know which part - that little nub between my legs.<br>"You need to get better locks," Horse said casually. "It took me about ten seconds to get in here."</i><br>~He breaks in and you're horny again. Forget the saying having to do with guys thinking with the wrong head. Apparently, dumb women are capable of the same thing.<br><br><i>"I'm in charge here, don't forget it," he stated.<br>I nodded, mesmerized.</i><br>~lalalalalalalalala. I'm in my happy place, humming a tune right now. Anything to make the pain go away.<br><br><i>I didn't think he had a girlfriend but we hadn't actually talked about it. Probably should have asked that before grabbing his dick in the pool.</i><br>~Nah. Because that would have required thinking about something other than sex.<br><br><i>My anger disappeared, replaced with terrible unease. I'd forgotten how terrifying this could be.</i><br>~You get the point.<br><br>I could go on and on. She finally stands up to him in one scene which had me cheering, then she went and started spamming him with "can we talk?" texts. Co-dependency is a bitch, apparently. And don't even get me started about how a near-rape experience with another person was glossed over in favor of more sexual tension. Sigh. <br><br><b>But I'm not giving this book 1 star for the following reasons :</b><br><br>1. When I wasn't screaming at Marie, I was entertained by the story. I like reading about MC life. Organized clubs and gangs have always fascinated me. <br><br>2. I actually liked a lot of the characters other than Marie. Picnic is one of the characters who I'm rooting for to find a HEA. I also want to see Picnic's daughter break out and find a life of her own. <br><br>3. The writing was decent. The author can tell a good story. Since my main frustration did not revolve around the club life aspect, I think that I might enjoy reading other books in this series with a different take on a female lead. They can't all be Marie, right? At least I'm hoping *cross fingers*<br><br>4. The old ladies were an entertaining bunch. Sisterhood can be fun to read about.<br><br>5. This quote : <i>"It's a .38," he said proudly. "I know you're a .22 girl, but it's time for us to take the next step in our relationship."</i><br><br>6. I felt like Horse was honestly willing to try and change his ways. We don't always get to see this in books. Sometimes the men go for a lukewarm compromise. In this case, the man did actually make the effort to try and be worthy of the woman he loved. It came later than I would have liked to have seen but at least it happened. <br><br><br><br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6023710540211346803">What in the <b>FUCK</b> did I just read? <br/><br/>Did I read about a man named Horse who's hung like a horse? <b>Yes.</b><br/><br/>An Alpha bad ass mofo biker? <b>Yes.</b> <br/><br/>A heroine named Marie who doesn't know her way in the biker world but somehow becomes a badass herself. <b>Yes.</b><br/><br/>Did I get so caught up in the story and characters that when it ended I had to use my left hand to stop my right hand pointer from sliding the page on my kindle cause my brain didn't connect to said pointer that the book ended? <b>Yes.</b><br/><br/>Did I love it? <b>You bet your </b></span>
  <span id="freeText6023710540211346803" style="display:none">What in the <b>FUCK</b> did I just read? <br /><br />Did I read about a man named Horse who's hung like a horse? <b>Yes.</b><br /><br />An Alpha bad ass mofo biker? <b>Yes.</b> <br /><br />A heroine named Marie who doesn't know her way in the biker world but somehow becomes a badass herself. <b>Yes.</b><br /><br />Did I get so caught up in the story and characters that when it ended I had to use my left hand to stop my right hand pointer from sliding the page on my kindle cause my brain didn't connect to said pointer that the book ended? <b>Yes.</b><br /><br />Did I love it? <b>You bet your sweet butt I did!</b><br /><br />This book is not only about Marie and Horse. It's also about family and their family dynamics. Marie and her problems with soon to be ex husband, her brother and her relationship with her mother who's in jail. Horse and his biker family The Reapers and their lifestyle. We get to meet some of them and their old ladies and sweet butts. They're funny, serious and love to have a great time. There's also a heartbreaking story with one couple that did bring tears to my eyes. Each character brings the story together either with their stupidity, personalities and betrayals and bantering.<br /><br />We do get Marie and Horse's POV's which I enjoyed. Their chemistry is instant and Marie is hesitant on their first encounter, leaving Horse with a case of blue balls. When they finally come together and when they get together its explosive. There's rough sex, sweet love making, angry sex, anal play which leaves to anal sex and voyeurism. There are some situations that some readers might find cring worthy but the author did a well job with said situations. The story flows perfectly that you do not want to leave the Reaper world.<br /><br />Loved the epilogue. Loved it!<br /><br />Favorite lines/moments:<br /><br /><i>"So why are you called Horse?"<br />"Cause I'm hung like one," he replied, smirking.<br /><br />Only my mother would end up finding love by trying to run over two cops. Clearly, John Benson was an idiot.<br /><br />"Fuck, this is gonna piss you off and then you aren't gonna let me stick my dick in you," he muttered.<br />"Do you have to be so crude?" I snapped. <br />"Have you met me?"<br /><br />Hid dick approved. It wanted to squeeze between those boobs and shoot out a pretty pearl necklace for her to wear.</i> <b>It's crude but I loved that line.</b><br /><br /><i>"Jerk." <br />"Hot piece of ass."<br />"Don't call me that!"<br />"I was referring to myself," he replied<br /><br />"She'd gone all Pulp Fiction on us, ready to defend you by killing all of us if she had to. Crouched over your body like Wonder Woman. Gives me a boner just thinking about it."<br /><br />"Jesus Christ...Thank fuck for that," Picnic said. "Nope, not Jesus, just a man," Horse whispered. "Although when women see my dick for the first time, they've been known to fall down on their knees and worship me."<br /><br />"Marie Caroline Jensen, will you do me the honor of being my permanent bitch?"<br />I smacked him on the side of his head as he burst out laughing...</i><br /><br /><b>*I'll be pimping this book for a long ass time*</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10578353294081137206"><br/><b>Hello, readers!!!!<br/><br/><br/>Let me introduce you all to Horse...</b><br/><p>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405414ra/789727.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</p><b>Well, not this kind of horse!<br/><br/>More like this kind of Horse...</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405414i/789728._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The kind that's handsome, like movie star handsome...<br/><br/>The kind that has dark hair, broad shoulders and muscular arms filled with tattoos... the <i>biker</i> kind.<br/><br/>And the reason they call him Horse? That's simple...because he's hung like one. <br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Oh my god... <br/><br/>It was huge. I mean, huge. Not just long, but thick and hard and flushed bright red so it looked almost angry. It curved up, w</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText10578353294081137206" style="display:none"><br><b>Hello, readers!!!!<br><br><br>Let me introduce you all to Horse...</b><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405414ra/789727.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><b>Well, not this kind of horse!<br><br>More like this kind of Horse...</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405414i/789728._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The kind that's handsome, like movie star handsome...<br><br>The kind that has dark hair, broad shoulders and muscular arms filled with tattoos... the <i>biker</i> kind.<br><br>And the reason they call him Horse? That's simple...because he's hung like one. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Oh my god... <br><br>It was huge. I mean, huge. Not just long, but thick and hard and flushed bright red so it looked almost angry. It curved up, wider in the center of the shaft before narrowing under the ridge of his head."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Well, <i>this</i> Horse has his eyes fixated on the pretty, innocent young girl named Marie...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405414i/789729._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>And when Horse wants something, everyone knows he always gets it...</i>
</b><br><br>The story starts when Jeff, Marie's brother, who's working for the Reaper's Motorcycle Club, decides to steal from the club and to gamble away the money. Soon the bikers find out about Jeff's stealing and, off course, they can't let him get away with doing something like that without paying for it...<br><br>And so Marie comes in the picture... Horse is immediately drawn to her in a way he's never been drawn to a woman before. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Someday," he whispered softly in my ear. "I don't want to hurt you. Not until you're ready for me... But someday I'm going to own all of you, Marie. You're all mine, babe. Knew it the first time I saw you. Couldn't give you up if I tried."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>As a way of letting Jeff pay for what he did, Horse convinces the other club members, to take Marie as "collateral" until Jeff finds a way to earn back the money so he can pay off his debt. And so, Marie is forced to join Horse and live with him, so she can temporarily become his "property".<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"This pussy is mine. You are mine. I'll fuck you when and where I want, and you can either take it or get the fuck out. Are we clear?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Yes, Horse could be very possessive, controlling and rude at times but at other moments, it showed that underneath it all, he was actually a pretty smart guy with a small heart; and along the way I really started to like him...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I want you to be my old lady, babe. That's all I have to offer. I'm a Reaper, and this is my world. You wear my patch, you be my woman and I'll be your man. We take the good times together and fight through the bad times. No games. That's everything I've got and it's all yours if you'll take it."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405414i/789730.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I will not tell you much more about the storyline, because that would spoil "the ride" for those who haven't read the story yet. What I would like to add, is that although the setting of the story reminded me a bit of the one in <i>Undeniable</i>, <i>Reaper's Property</i> was filled with much less drama and the "ugliness" in life. The women weren't constantly called "b*tches" and I also really liked that Horse <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[unlike, Deuce in Undeniable, didn't cheat on Marie. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> So for those who found Undeniable a little too "overwhelming", I think <i>Reaper's Property</i> certainly might be a much more suitable read.<br><br><br>All in all, I very much enjoyed reading <i>Reaper's Property</i>... It was a fun, entertaining story with some very hot scenes in it. The characters had funny names (going from Cookie to Bam-Bam to Picnic and at last but not least...Horse) and seeing as Sons of Anarchy sort of made me became a fan of the whole bad-ass biker world, I really liked getting to know even more about the bikers' way of life and their very unique way of handling things... <br><br><br><br><br><br><blockquote>*****</blockquote><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12974771582591700915">|DNF at 48%|<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif' width='500' height='245' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>“I don’t give a damn if you never wear panties again, but I know women are weird about that. Here’s the compromise. I’m gonna buy you new shit, but only shit I like. You’re gonna wear it until I pull it off to fuck you. Everyone wins.”</b><br/><br/>Yes, ladies and gentlemen, that's how it went.<br/><br/>I really <i>really</i> wanted to read and love this book. Why? Well, I needed some badass bikers action. <u>Sons Of Anarchy</u> left me with this void and I was craving for something awesome like that.<br/><br/>Sadly, this was not </span>
  <span id="freeText12974771582591700915" style="display:none">|DNF at 48%|<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420429845ra/13223235.gif" width="500" height="245" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“I don’t give a damn if you never wear panties again, but I know women are weird about that. Here’s the compromise. I’m gonna buy you new shit, but only shit I like. You’re gonna wear it until I pull it off to fuck you. Everyone wins.”</b><br><br>Yes, ladies and gentlemen, that's how it went.<br><br>I really <i>really</i> wanted to read and love this book. Why? Well, I needed some badass bikers action. <u>Sons Of Anarchy</u> left me with this void and I was craving for something awesome like that.<br><br>Sadly, this was not it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425518990i/13901436.gif" width="485" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is not going to be a long review, because it won't be a review. I just want to share with you why this book wasn't my cup of tea and why I feel like I need to sleep for 3 days so my eyes can, somehow, forget this thing.<br><br><i>And I'm sorry if this is your favorite book or you just love it. I tried.</i><br><br>Also, I want to let you know that I don't know what happens at the end of this book. I don't know if things get better but right now I just can't bring myself to care. I will only talk about what I read.<br><br>If there's something I hate more than an abusive man is a dumb-ass woman. That's it. You know, there's a lot of women fighting for themselves, there are a lot of badass female characters, women of honor but Marie is not one of them.<br><br>I tried to be on her side, really. I tried to see things from a psychological aspect, you know, maybe she was still in some kind of shock, maybe she felt guilty or like shit, maybe she was confused and took the first male attention she got, maybe she thought that she deserved what she got and I know she lef her husband but I just... <br><br>I tried to think of Marie as a victim, because clearly she must have been nuts to jump from one abusive relationship to another. And before you tell me it was all consensual, I know that. I also know Horse cares about Marie but <i>still.</i> One would think: uhm, you know, I did nothing with my life and now I can. I can put all that ugliness behind me and start over. I can save money and go to culinary school. I can do stuff for <b>myself.</b> That's not how Marie's brain operates so I cannot say she's a victim or that she's confused so I can only say she's just plain stupid.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425231029ra/13865141.gif" width="400" height="202" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then we have Horse.<br><br>I have no words for him.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424364501ra/13752248.gif" width="450" height="253" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The only way I tolerated the guys this long was because I was picturing Jason Momoa while reading. Not kidding at all.<br><br>I went from:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425518990ra/13901437.gif" width="500" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>to:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425231029ra/13865140.gif" width="450" height="254" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Because I can't respect a man or a person who thinks like this:<br><br><b>"If she left him, he’d hunt her down and drag her back home by the hair if he had to."</b> but says <i> “You’re with me of your own free will..."</i> HA! Hypocrite much?<br><br>I love an alpha man. I love when they take control. I adore reading them but there's a big difference between being an alpha man and being an abusive bastard. He might not hit her but he plays with her and treats her like an object. Call me softy if you want but I can tolerate and enjoy all kind of thing in bed and I usually don't mind at all dirty words but Horse was just nasty in and outside the bedroom. <br><br>And don't get me started with those <i>sweet moments</i> when he showed how much he cares about Marie because all I could think about was when a man who's hitting his woman gives her flowers or pats her damned head after the beating. Fucking sick.<br><br>Seriously, I was just annoyed and I felt rather insulted. And frustrated because there were parts of the books that held my attention but it wasn't enough.<br><br>And I don't feel confortable rating this book since I didn't finish it.<br><br>Like I said I'm sorry because I really wanted to like this book like y'all but yeah, that didn't happen.<br><br><s>I wish someone just...</s><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425518990ra/13901438.gif" width="312" height="234" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_510526310" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/510526310" />
    <a title="Auntee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/886675-auntee"><img alt="Auntee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281897695p2/886675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/510526310?book_show_action=true">Jan 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Auntee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Auntee" href="/user/show/886675-auntee">Auntee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781419970290" href="/book/show/18731345-reaper-s-property">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of erotic romance in the style of Kristen Ashley</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=for_my_kindle">for_my_kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=e-books">e-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=dirty-talker">dirty-talker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=2013_reads">2013_reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=overly-endowed">overly-endowed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=once-more">once-more</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer510526310" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10503289017272823085"><b>Reading once more...there's a lot I forgot</b><br/><br/>I don't think I'm destined to write a review for this one because...*big sigh*...the power just went off for 30 minutes (on the coldest night of the year)...but now that it's back on I guess I'll make an attempt to get my thoughts on paper.<br/><br/>If I could sum up this story in one sentence I'd say something like...<i>
  <b>"Ohh, mama!"</b>
</i><br/><br/>I was urged to read this one by my GR friends because of its similarity to Kristen Ashley's <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13448656.Motorcycle_Man__Dream_Man___4_' title='Motorcycle Man (Dream Man, #4) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Motorcycle Man</a>. And yes, there are some </span>
  <span id="freeText10503289017272823085" style="display:none"><b>Reading once more...there's a lot I forgot</b><br><br>I don't think I'm destined to write a review for this one because...*big sigh*...the power just went off for 30 minutes (on the coldest night of the year)...but now that it's back on I guess I'll make an attempt to get my thoughts on paper.<br><br>If I could sum up this story in one sentence I'd say something like...<i>
  <b>"Ohh, mama!"</b>
</i><br><br>I was urged to read this one by my GR friends because of its similarity to Kristen Ashley's <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13448656.Motorcycle_Man__Dream_Man___4_" title="Motorcycle Man (Dream Man, #4) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Motorcycle Man</a>. And yes, there are some similarities: both heroes are members of motorcycle clubs; both heroes are big bad alphas; both heroes are highly sexual; both heroes are blunt, sexy, dirty talkers. Both stories are told in first person from the heroine's POV, <i>although</i> <b>Reaper's Property</b> is also told in third person and we get to hear the hero's thoughts (which I appreciated).<br><br><i>Our hero, "Horse" (as in "hung-like-a"...)</i><br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=fabricio-1-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380405775i/790975.jpg" alt="fabricio-1" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But there are differences. <b>Reaper's</b> is much darker in tone; the hero is darker, he's into illegal/shady stuff (although exactly what is not spelled out--it's "club business" whenever the heroine asks questions--meaning MYOB). <b>Reaper's</b> doesn't go into as much detail as a KA novel--it's much faster paced and dare I say the editing is better. This fast pace made it hard to put down--there really wasn't a good place to stop reading! But enough about the comparisons.<br><br>I really enjoyed reading this. At first I was a little put off by just how bold and dirty talkin' the hero was. Some of the things he said were just so audacious...but then I had to laugh! I really enjoyed the relationship between 30 yr. old, former Marine Horse (yeah, that's his name, and for the obvious reason) and Marie (given the nickname "Sweet butt", which she hated). If you can get past a hero named "Horse" (really, I wish the heroine would've referred to him by his given name--Marcus) which is really kind of ridiculous (maybe he's a distant relative of "The Cannon" from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/3228418.Devil_s_Pact__The_Devil_s_Playground__1_" title="Devil's Pact (The Devil's Playground #1) by Samantha Cruise" rel="nofollow noopener">Devil's Pact</a>?)...but I digress.<br><br>Anyway, here's just a sample of some of the Neanderthal things Horse utters (just to get the heroine all riled up):<br><br><i>
  <b>"Your brother's lucky, because I wanna stick my dick in you more than I wanna kill him. Otherwise this wouldn't be worth the trouble."<br><br>"This pussy," Horse said, fingering her roughly. "This pussy is mine. You are mine. I'll f*** you when and where I want, and you can either take it or get the f*** out. Are we clear?"<br><br>"I told you before, this is</b>
</i> my <i>
  <b>pussy," he continued, softly but with a hint of threat too. "I f*** you, nobody else does. Which hole I f*** is up for negotiation."</b>
</i><br><br>Yes, Horse can be a real badass, but believe it or not, he does have a softer, vulnerable, kind of sweet side. I don't think I would've enjoyed this one much if I didn't see evidence of this side. I guess I can admit that I found him (and the whole Reaper's world) kind of fascinating...even though there's no way on God's green earth I could <i>ever</i> imagine myself living that life!<br><br>I enjoyed Marie too. I like how she stood up to Horse; I loved how passionate they were together--they certainly did everything with a passion. They loved hard, they argued hard. I'm sure they never had a boring day in their whole relationship. Marie was a little young and she made some mistakes in life (maybe she trusted her skeezy brother a little too much, but she was loyal to the core to him), but I think she learned from her mistakes and was on her way to being a more mature, grounded person.<br><br>There were some things I would've liked the author to include. Just a little more about Horse's background (although I did appreciate the little backstory about his time in the Marines; and the interaction with his sister). There were some dangling threads--<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[what happened to Max when he tried to rape Marie; what happened to Marie's ex when Horse paid him a visit; what happened to Marie after she killed Max in self-defense--we know she gets off, but the story skips ahead to months later. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> These were just minor quibbles though. This story really kept me turning the pages. Between the outrageousness of the storyline and the wild and crazy relationship between Horse and Marie, I found I just couldn't get enough. I laughed, I gasped, I smiled. I shook my head a time or two; I even teared up near the end. If you're looking for a story with <i>plenty</i> of hot, any-which-way-you-can sex, plenty of crazy action, a H/h who live life passionately, and enough detail and inventive storytelling to keep you turning the pages, then give this book a try. I dare you not to fall just <i>a little</i> in love with Horse and Marie...I know that I did! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>
    <b>"Marie Caroline Jensen, will you do me the honor of being my permanent bitch?"</b>
  </i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Aww... 4 1/2 stars<br><br><i>Warning: This book contains explicit sex (including oral and anal); near public sex; graphic language; a dirty-talkin' hero; and violence. Not for the faint of heart.</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <span id="freeText8690884791013373193" style="display:none"><b>ETA: 3/8 - Horse's POV short: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://totallybookedblog.com/2013/03/08/sticky-sweet-a-tb-exclusive-horse-pov-short-story-and-interview-with-joanna-wylde-plus-giveaway/">http://totallybookedblog.com/2013/03/...</a></b><br><br><br><br>Kudos to Joanna Wylde for coming up with a name like "Horse" for her bad@ss Alpha motorcycle male! Who could resist? I sure couldn't...and to set you up, here's how I see the infamous Horse:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1362163506p8/705916.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Phe<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www...okay">www...okay</a>, back to the story (if I can focus!)...<br><br>Horse sees girl. <br>Horse wants girl.<br>Horse takes girl. <br>The end. <br><br>Well, almost but no, really, that is it essentially with a few major drama scenes and <i>whooo hooo</i> steamy sex scenes. Hey, he wasn't nicknamed Horse for nothing!! And he's very proud of himself for living up to that. <br><br>I really enjoy these type of books that have scenes that take you past your comfort zone and while this one wasn't as intense as <i>Undeniable</i> (by Madeline Sheehan), it still managed to hook me and I could not put it down. <br><br>I love reading about two people that just seem right for each other but there's some reason it's hard for them to get together. Understandably, Marie is not from the motorcycle gang lifestyle and she is really oblivious! There are some really funny scenes where she just doesn't get it but it also endears her to you. I like that she put herself out there and tried to acclimate to their environment and for the most part, she learned and grew. However, there was a part at the end, where she didn't learn. Granted, it made for some good drama but it did seemed a bit out of character. <br><br>Back to Horse...the one problem I had is that I never got why he wanted Marie so much and why he fell in love with her. I get that he thought she was hot (especially with a gun!), he liked her cooking and fighting with her but I was hoping that we would get more of the why especially with having his POV. (which was fantastic!) I also loved that Horse was more than just a sex machine but that he had a good mind and was the accountant for the club. (The dummy ledgers were perfect!!)<br><br>And I loved all the drama. It's always great seeing the Alpha male get jealous as well as the heroine. I'm glad that JW reined things in though and she just pushed things a bit. <br><br>There are a lot of other great characters. I really loved the relationship between Marie and Jeff (her brother). I wished things would have worked out differently. And thank goodness for the other "old ladies" taking care of Marie...she really needed them. There are a plethora of characters that JW could keep on writing about and I wouldn't mind at all. In fact, I would LOVE it. <div id="review_509061707" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/509061707" />
    <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish"><img alt="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398981306p2/1113032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/509061707?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781419944673" href="/book/show/17229454-reaper-s-property">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish by: </span>
      Michele ~ la Smoocherina
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=badass-biker-dudes">badass-biker-dudes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=format-kindle-or-kindle-compatible">format-kindle-or-kindle-compatible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=own-have-read">own-have-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=first-in-series-trilogy-duet">first-in-series-trilogy-duet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=2013-reads">2013-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=buddy-read-kaasg">buddy-read-kaasg</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=motorcycle-club">motorcycle-club</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer509061707" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12831695623533788312"><br/><i>Reaper’s Property</i> is, from what I understand, the start to a new series centering on the Reapers Motorcycle Club. It’s an exciting, gritty, sexy story, one I enjoyed, start to finish.<blockquote><i>From the cover:</i><br/><br/>Marie doesn’t need a complication like Horse. The massive, tattooed, badass biker who shows up at her brother’s house one afternoon doesn’t agree. He wants Marie on his bike and in his bed. Now.<br/><br/>But Marie just left her abusive jerk of an ex-husband and she’s not looking for a new man. Especially one li</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText12831695623533788312" style="display:none"><br /><i>Reaper’s Property</i> is, from what I understand, the start to a new series centering on the Reapers Motorcycle Club. It’s an exciting, gritty, sexy story, one I enjoyed, start to finish.<blockquote><i>From the cover:</i><br /><br />Marie doesn’t need a complication like Horse. The massive, tattooed, badass biker who shows up at her brother’s house one afternoon doesn’t agree. He wants Marie on his bike and in his bed. Now.<br /><br />But Marie just left her abusive jerk of an ex-husband and she’s not looking for a new man. Especially one like Horse—she doesn’t know his real name or where he lives, she’s ninety percent certain he’s a criminal and that the “business” he talks with her brother isn’t website design. She needs him out of her life, which would be a snap if he’d just stop giving her mind-blowing orgasms.<br /><br />Horse is part of the Reapers Motorcycle Club, and when he wants something, he takes it. What he wants is Marie, but she’s not interested in becoming “property of”.<br /><br />Then her brother steals from the club. Marie can save him by giving Horse what he wants—at home, in public, on his bike… If she’s a very, very good girl, she’ll get lots more of those orgasms only he can offer, and he’ll let her brother live.<br /><br />Maybe.</blockquote>I’ve seen a lot of rave reviews for this book, comparing it to Kristen Ashley’s writing, so being the KA Addict I am, I just had to see what all the hype was about. The story starts out strong, grabbed hold and kept me turning the pages as, in flashbacks, we’re given the details that lead up to where the story begins – in Jeff and Marie’s living room, Jeff on his knees with a gun held to his head by a bad-ass biker. <br /><br />I enjoyed the writing, and I enjoyed the plot, but I felt like there were some holes, things I needed to know about to truly feel like the story was resolved, and to accept Horse and Marie's <i>happily ever after.</i> <br /><br />I'll break it down. These are serious spoilers, so DO NOT CLICK unless you've read the book. <br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ 1. I want to know what kind of punishment Max got for trying to rape Marie. That's a huge infraction right there, so what happened to him? He was only away a couple months - was short term banishment his punishment? Or did Horse beat the shit out of him, as I would have expected? I mean, really, that's a huge crime. HUGE! Honestly, I'm not sure why Max was still breathing, let alone welcomed back to the club. I need more information on that.<br /><br />2. I don't like the whole second, secret email address thing. The way the club was monitoring her, the way they were looking for their leak - they weren't too bright if they didn't catch that. And about that... did she ever come clean to Horse? I don't like the lies, the sneaking around. I mean, I do get why she did it, but once she found out that her brother wasn’t being honest, when she discovered what he was up to… she had to see that she’d been duped. So, was she upfront with Horse, who nearly died trying to rescue her? For me to believe they have a solid relationship, a relationship built on trust, those things needed to be worked out where I could see them. I didn't get a true soul mate feeling between Horse and Marie, and this is, in part, why.<br /><br />3. I would have liked the epilogue to include details about how Marie managed to get away with murder. Yeah, the MC got her an attorney, but she still had blood all over her, two dead, and one mostly dead, bodies... how was all that explained? Again, this is huge!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />And a side note: Because I keep hearing the Kristen Ashley comparisons, I want to add my 2 cents. This is just my opinion but, apart from edgy bad-ass biker dudes, I didn’t see much similarity to Kristen Ashley’s writing. Their writing style is different, the way they tell the story is different… the similarities – again, just my opinion – are only found in the plot props - the harsh world of a motorcycle club.<br /><br />So yeah… while I <i>really</i> enjoyed <i>Reaper’s Property</i>, there are just too many questions left in my mind to give me that 'wrapped up nice and tidy' feeling I like in my books. But make no mistakes, the writing is good, the world this author has created is exciting, the characters are bad-ass alpha males and I adored them. Ms. Wylde is a talented writer and I’m definitely looking forward to reading more in this series.<br /><br />3.5/5 stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="12831695623533788312" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1693914962" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1693914962" />
    <a title="Clumsy Storyteller " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21493936-clumsy-storyteller"><img alt="Clumsy Storyteller " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1542204051p2/21493936.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1693914962?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Clumsy Storyteller " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Clumsy Storyteller " href="/user/show/21493936-clumsy-storyteller">Clumsy Storyteller </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<div id="review_512767242" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/512767242?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781419944673" href="/book/show/17229454-reaper-s-property">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer512767242" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9553690777596220912"><b> 5 ‘HUGE’ Stars ;-) </b><br/><br/>  I <u>loved</u> this book! A big thanks to my many gr friends that raved about this one and got me to bump it way up on my tbr list! The very best part about this book... <b>HORSE</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Horse was dangerous. I could smell it on him. Seriously. Under the delicious scent of leather, light sweat, and man was a pungent strain of pure trouble.</i>
</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&current=ReapersProperty_horse.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406103i/791857.jpg' alt='HORSE- Reaper's Propertyy' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>Even scary, the man made my panties wet.</b><br/><br/>This story starts off with a lady named Marie. Marie has just moved in with her brother Jeff, after her lying</span>
  <span id="freeText9553690777596220912" style="display:none"><b> 5 ‘HUGE’ Stars ;-) </b><br><br>  I <u>loved</u> this book! A big thanks to my many gr friends that raved about this one and got me to bump it way up on my tbr list! The very best part about this book... <b>HORSE</b><br><br><b>
  <i>Horse was dangerous. I could smell it on him. Seriously. Under the delicious scent of leather, light sweat, and man was a pungent strain of pure trouble.</i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&amp;current=ReapersProperty_horse.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406103i/791857.jpg" alt="HORSE- Reaper's Propertyy" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>Even scary, the man made my panties wet.</b><br><br>This story starts off with a lady named Marie. Marie has just moved in with her brother Jeff, after her lying, cheating, sob of a husband starts abusing her. Jeff is living a few towns away in the trailer he and Marie grew up in. Their mom is currently in jail, so it is just Marie and Jeff. Marie gets a job at a daycare and is trying to get back on her feet. Jeff is working for a Motorcycle Club called The Reapers. <br>One day, Marie is hanging out in the yard, wearing her bikini top and jamming to Def Lepord’s ‘Pour some sugar on me’, when three bikes pull up her driveway. Here is where she meets Horse.<br><br><b>
  <i>”So, why are you called Horse?” <br>“Cause’ I’m hung like one.”</i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&amp;current=ReapersProperty-hunglikehorse.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406103i/791858.jpg" alt="Reapers Property" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>It was huge. I mean huge.</b><br> <b>
  <i> “Told you thats why they call me Horse."</i>
</b>  <br><br>Marie and Horse have chemistry. It’s pretty evident, even from their first meeting. She has never been this attracted to a man, and there is something about Marie... Horse is drawn to her. He even loves her bitchy attitude towards him.<br><br><b>
  <i> “I’ve never ridden on a bike before.” Horse leaned over and gave me a quick kiss on the mouth. “Lookin’ forward to being your first, babe.”</i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&amp;current=ReapersProperty-bike.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406103i/791859.jpg" alt="Reapers Propoerty" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>Don’t give me that shit,” he growled. “I can get laid whenever I want, I don’t have to drive four hundred miles round trip to get off. Women see the bike, they see the tats and the cut, they’re all over that shit.”</i>
</b><br><br>Horse and Marie continue to hang out and start seeing each other more. After a few misunderstandings, they stop. <br>Meanwhile, Marie’s brother Jeff (not the brightest crayon in the box) has been making some big mistakes with the MC’s money. Mistakes that could easily get him killed. Horse saves his ass for one reason only. Marie. The Reapers will spare his life and give him time make things right, but Horse gets Marie. Marie would do anything to save her brother, so she goes with Horse. Horse wants to sleep with Marie, of course, but he also want to own her, to have her as his Old Lady, to be his property...<br><b>
  <i> “I want you to be my old lady, babe. That all I have to offer. I’m a Reaper, and this is my world. You wear my patch, you be my woman and I’ll be your man. We’ll take the good times together and fight through the bad times. No games. That everything I’ve got and its all yours if you’ll take it.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>Oh Horse.... </b> Badass biker, alpha male, can be rude and crude, offensive even at times, but he is sexy as hell and completely lovable! We have a hot biker guy that is actually faithful to his woman? Hot damn! That makes him that much hotter! Some of the things that came out of that mans mouth... made me swoon!<br><b>
  <i> “I’m not gonna let you go, Marie. I’m keeping you and I don’t care if I go to hell for doing it. I don’t care about anything except fucking you.”<br>“Someday I’m going to own all of you, Marie. You’re all mine, babe. Knew it the first time I saw you. Couldn’t give you up if I tried.”</i>
</b><br><br>Marie was a strong woman. She didn’t have an easy life, but she tried. She loved her family and was a loyal woman. She wasn’t afraid to speak her mind. Most of the time I really liked her. She frustrated me at times, but overall she was cool in my book. I loved all the ‘old ladies’! Those women were awesome! <br><br>If you are looking for something hot to read... Marie and Horse had some heat between them! There are some intense, hot and sexy scenes in this book! Panties... be prepared to melt. <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&amp;current=Reapersproperty-thatshot.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406103ra/791860.gif" alt="Thats hot..." class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Reaper’s Property was a fantastic read! Fun, sexy, and extremely entertaining! Loved me some Horse! My only complaint, is that I feel towards the end <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[after Bagger’s funeral, going with Max to meet her brother, and the injuries etc <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> it felt a little rushed, with we had more time at the end to find more out! The epilogue was great! If you haven’t read this one, you are really missing out! GET TO IT!!!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="9553690777596220912" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" href="/user/show/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha">SueBee★bring me an alpha!★</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer555828584" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14724761158453541678"><b>★★★★★! Reaper’s Property, book 1 (stand-alone), Introducing Horse; tall, larger-than-life, movie-star handsome biker and everything that is sex with him.</b><br/><br/>Horse’s and Marie’s story comes to pass when Marie’s brother, Jeff who had been hired by the Reaper’s MC club ends up stealing from the club. They offer Marie her brother’s life and his chance to make good on the theft in exchange for her going to live with Horse. The book follows Marie and Horse in the events leading up to that point and then t</span>
  <span id="freeText14724761158453541678" style="display:none"><b>★★★★★! Reaper’s Property, book 1 (stand-alone), Introducing Horse; tall, larger-than-life, movie-star handsome biker and everything that is sex with him.</b><br /><br />Horse’s and Marie’s story comes to pass when Marie’s brother, Jeff who had been hired by the Reaper’s MC club ends up stealing from the club. They offer Marie her brother’s life and his chance to make good on the theft in exchange for her going to live with Horse. The book follows Marie and Horse in the events leading up to that point and then the story continues from there.<br /><br /><b>Below is the link for “Sticky Sweet” (Reaper’s MC, #0.5)</b><br />Their first meeting from Horse’s POV. <u>I recommend reading after chapter 1 of Reaper’s Property.</u><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://joannawylde.net/styled/styled-3/index.html">http://joannawylde.net/styled/styled-...</a><br /><br /><b>Hero: <u>Marcus Antonius Caesar McDonnell, “Horse”</u>/30 years old/ex-marine - biker - Reaper’s MC member - accountant/black hair/green eyes/6’6”<br />Heroine: <u> “Marie Caroline Jensen</u>/25 years old/childcare worker/separated/dark brown hair/5’4”</b><br /><br />Story is mostly told from Marie’s POV, but every once in awhile we get Horse’s POV (in 3rd person).<br /><br />At first glance Horse has so many of the superficial qualities I like in a hero… sinfully good looks:<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Tall, built, with shoulder-length hair he kept pulled back in a ponytail, and thick black stubble on his face. Stark, tribal cuffs ringed his wrists and upper arms. And what a face… Horse was handsome, like movie star handsome.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />And he is very well endowed:<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“So why are you called Horse?” <br />“’Cause I’m hung like one,” he replied, smirking.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />But we soon learn that there are many more layers to Horse. He is this hard, strong and fierce biker, but he is also this soft, sweet and kind man. He is smart, working as an accountant handling the clubs complex finances. And he is funny:<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Glad you like it.” “What?” I asked, confused. <br />“My body,” he replied, smirking. “It’s the only one you get to look at or f~ck, so it’s good the package works for you.” I blushed fiercely…”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Marie was both naive and annoying which is often the case when paired with a larger-than-life hero. But she is also sweet, kind and loyal and she is reflective, insightful and she is trying to make a new life for herself:<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“… while it might not have been a picture-perfect childhood, it hadn’t been too bad for a couple of white-trash kids whose dad took off before they hit grade school.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />And just like Horse she has her funny moments:<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I blinked at him, dazed. “Gonna f~ck you now.” <br />“Sure,” I whispered, dazed. “Not sure I’m gonna be able to participate too much, think you blew a circuit or something.”<br /><br />***<br />Horse: What do you think? Gotta go, church in a few <br />Me: Church?!?? Didn’t peg you for a church kind of guy <br />Horse: What we call a club meeting. I try to stay away from collection plates <br />Me: Don’t get holy water in your beer!</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />For me this story offers it all, starting with a glimpse into the Reaper’s MC club life:<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Remember, we’re a tribe. We live together, we die together and what’s ours is ours. When times are good, we’re all good. Bad times, we may eat shit but we eat it together. Most people can’t handle that level of commitment.”<br /><br />***<br />“We’re men—one percenters. F~cking kings of the MC world. We don’t follow the rules, we make our own goddamn rules.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Many of Reaper’s members were veterans and this story is also a stark reminder of our many heroes who never came home:<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“He’s Freebird chapter now and he doesn’t need his patches anymore. It’s time to send them back to him. We won’t forget. Reapers forever, forever Reapers.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />And this is of course very much an erotic tale about Horse and Marie and everything that is mind-blowing sex with Horse:<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I’m in charge here, don’t forget it,” he stated. I nodded, mesmerized.”<br /><br />***<br />“I have no idea how long it was before Horse came, because I was floating in my own little world. He collapsed on top of me, managing to keep enough of his weight to one side that he didn’t crush me. Our breathing slowed. Then he leaned up on one elbow, sliding me so we lay face-to-face.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />Horse may have brought Marie on the pretense of collateral, but there is a budding love story giving as a glimpse into the other, softer side of Horse:<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“But someday I’m going to own all of you, Marie. You’re all mine, babe. Knew it the first time I saw you. Couldn’t give you up if I tried.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><br />In addition there is suspense, the intrigue and mystery will keep you at the edge of your seat until the very last page. I will say no more. You need to read this story yourself!<br /><br />All in all an excellent read, great character development of both Horse and Marie. In their story you will also meet many interesting side characters, some who most likely will be featured in the next-coming books. <br /><br />***<br />Hero rating: 5 stars <br />Heroine rating: 3.5 stars<br />Sex scenes rating: 5 stars<br />Sex scenes frequency: 5 stars<br />Storyline concept rating: 5 stars<br />Storytelling skills rating: 5 stars<br />Story ending rating: 5 stars<br />Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 4.5 stars<br />************************************************<br /><b>Overall rating: 5 stars<br /><br />Would I recommend this book: Yes.<br />Would I re-read this book: Maybe later.<br />Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="14724761158453541678" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

Since I have the mentality of a 12 year old I just laughed and laughed forever at that. <br><br>This one isn’t for the weak, so if you are of the butthurt generation don’t say I didn’t warn you. The premise behind <i>Reaper’s Property</i> is that Marie’s brother is a douchebag stoner idiot/‘puter genius who was hired to do some creative maneuvering of the motorcycle club’s funds and decided to skim off the top. D-bag brother finds himself $50,000 in the hole and zero method of paying back the debt. Enter Marie. Horse had his eye set on her becoming his “old lady,” but since she didn’t understand club lingo she told him to hit the bricks. Now that her brother’s life is on the line Marie has the chance to save him – by offering herself up as collateral. This is the part where you have to let reality go if you plan on enjoying the ride . . . <br><br><b>
  <i>“Glad you like it.”<br><br>“What?” I asked.<br><br>“My body,” he replied, smirking. “It’s the only one you get to look at or fuck, so it’s good the package works for you.”</i>
</b><br><br> <i>Reaper’s Property</i> wasn’t really my ideal cuppa for the simple fact that WHY THE EFF DIDN’T HORSE JUST TELL HER THE WHOLE INDENTURED SERVITUDE THING WAS A RUSE BECAUSE HE WANTED TO KEEP HER SAFE AND ALSO KINDA LURRRRRRVED HER AND MOST DEFINITELY WANTED TO MAKE ALL THE SEX WITH HER?!?!?!?!?! Stupid plot is stupid. However, if you can let your mind be free to the idea of some dumbshit sex robot type of woman who suffers the body betrayal B.S. anytime dude breathes near her, you’re probably in for a good time and will eventually be okay with the stupid ass plot too . . . <br><br><b>
  <i>“I don’t want to be your enemy,” he said firmly. “I want to be your man. You make me feel crazy things, Marie, and I don’t want to lose you.”</i>
</b><br><br>Or maybe that’s just me and I’ve been hypnotized by all of these longhaired motorbikers *shrug* . . . .<br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455132149ra/18060836.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<span id="freeTextContainer16492441212751825715">First of all I would like to apologize to anyone who stumbled upon my status updates during reading this book!<br/>Yes I know they were very spoliery (is that even a word?) but I just could not help myself! It was really stronger then me and I just had to share that with everyone!<br/><br/>I had so much fun reading this book! Oh my god I laughed like crazy!   <span id="freeText16492441212751825715" style="display:none">First of all I would like to apologize to anyone who stumbled upon my status updates during reading this book!<br>Yes I know they were very spoliery (is that even a word?) but I just could not help myself! I ran across this book on Facebook, read the blurb and just couldn’t say <i>no</i>. Come on you guys! Get this: The Hero is a tattooed, badass Alpha biker named Horse. That’s right, you heard me. <i>HORSE!</i> It took me a nano second for mind to come to an obvious and pervy conclusion and another minute to shuck $7 for this book. Was it worth it? Hells fuckin yea it was! <br><br><b>
  <i>“Someday,” he whispered softly in my ear. “I don’t want to hurt you. Not until you’re ready for me… But someday I’m going to own all of you, Marie. You’re all mine, babe. Knew it the first time I saw you. Couldn’t give you up if I tried.”</i>
</b><br><br>Marie just moved back into her brother, Jeff’s, house after leaving her no good cheating soon to be ex-husband. Marie adores and loves Jeff. So when he gets into some serious trouble with a local MC, The Reapers, she doesn’t hesitate to help him. Anything. <br><br><b>
  <i>“This is your option,” Horse said to me abruptly. “You want to keep dumbass alive, pack a bag and climb on my bike when we leave. </b><br><br>Just like sexy Rock Star books, I’ve also learned that I’m a sucker for Badass Biker books. To me, they are the epitome of what I love most about my Alpha Heroes: They’re strong, brooding, sexy, possessive, protective and have that <i>don’t fucking mess with me or my woman</i> attitude. Fucking swoon! If you’re a fan of Madeline Sheehan’s Undeniable, you will probably like this read. It’s not as good, nor as intense, but still a great read nonetheless. <br><br>-----<br><b>

  <span id="freeText12226479907131352703" style="display:none">I had two problems with this book; the heroine did a lot of slut-shaming, she spoke ill about women who had a lot of sex and showed bare skin, which I thought was despicable of her to do. <br /><br />One scene in particular that infuriated me was when she was watching a girl get gang-banged, and the girl was obviously enjoying getting fucked, but the heroine made some remarks about the scene that just turned my stomach. The girl wasn't being raped, she was having fun. So, can't women fuck as many men as they want without this heroine judging them for it?<br /><br />And it wasn't JUST the heroine doing the slut-shaming. Many women were looked down upon by a lot of other characters; "old ladies" and "men."<br /><br />And the other issue I had, was the time-jump. To avoid spoilers, I won't tell you what time jump I'm talking about, but read and you'll find out. <br /><br />Overall, I liked the two characters, the heroine annoyed me a bit, but not too much. The chemistry was lacking but it was fine at the end.</span>

There's one thing you have to know - if you call someone "horse" (konj) on my native language, you better be ready for fight because it's like telling someone he's a dumb fuck or something similar. First impression after five pages: "Oh, the white trash - excuse for being a big failure." I had some Sookie flashbacks. But then... the bikes. The boys.   function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('QhJGFo1dFTphKYrHp7QnCJOB6hkGNcDlgaHA1PZPIQ6ahcbYprK0oJ0a+PRTwV2vq0ZFMF6Ft2iJv8Vtk1cc0w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Xu10bTXfSsHvWwNejX5bMPi5xcJdnrTCJ48C2ilEmXyGevSjHjDrWxNocW15CyGXwH5q6wUuw08vkQdjTFykoQ==')})
  }
